public class SnesRom
{
	public void L000000()
	{
		Cpu.Break();
	}

	public void L008C3B_Reset()
	{
		I = 1;
		C = 0;
		C = 1; temp = C; C = E; E = temp;
		return this.L808C42_Start();
	}

	public void L7D00BC()
	{
		Cpu.Break();
	}

	public void L808202_WaitFor014B()
	{
		Stack.Push(P);
		Stack.Push(B);
		Stack.Push(K);
		B = Stack.Pop();
		P |= 0x30;
		A = 0x01;
		[0x014B] = A;
	}

	public void L80820D_Wait()
	{
		A = [0x014B];

		if (Z == 0)
			return this.L80820D_Wait();

		B = Stack.Pop();
		P = Stack.Pop();
		return;
	}

	public void L808215_EnableNMI()
	{
		Stack.Push(P);
		Stack.Push(B);
		Stack.Push(K);
		B = Stack.Pop();
		P |= 0x20;
		A = [0x013C];
		A |= 0x80;
		[0x4200] = A;
		[0x013C] = A;
		B = Stack.Pop();
		P = Stack.Pop();
		return;
	}

	public void L808229_DisableNMI()
	{
		Stack.Push(P);
		Stack.Push(B);
		Stack.Push(K);
		B = Stack.Pop();
		P |= 0x20;
		A = [0x013C];
		A &= 0x7F;
		[0x4200] = A;
		[0x013C] = A;
		B = Stack.Pop();
		P = Stack.Pop();
		return;
	}

	public void L80823D()
	{
		Stack.Push(P);
		Stack.Push(B);
		Stack.Push(K);
		B = Stack.Pop();
		P |= 0x20;
		A = [0x0100];
		A |= 0x80;
		[0x0100] = A;
		this.L808202_WaitFor014B();
		B = Stack.Pop();
		P = Stack.Pop();
		return;
	}

	public void L808252()
	{
		Stack.Push(P);
		Stack.Push(B);
		Stack.Push(K);
		B = Stack.Pop();
		P |= 0x20;
		A = [0x0100];
		A &= 0x7F;
		[0x0100] = A;
		this.L808202_WaitFor014B();
		B = Stack.Pop();
		P = Stack.Pop();
		return;
	}

	public void L80827B()
	{
		Stack.Push(P);
		Stack.Push(B);
		Stack.Push(K);
		B = Stack.Pop();
		P |= 0x20;
		A = [0x013C];
		A &= 0xEF;
		[0x4200] = A;
		[0x013C] = A;
		B = Stack.Pop();
		P = Stack.Pop();
		return;
	}

	public void L8082A3()
	{
		Stack.Push(P);
		Stack.Push(B);
		Stack.Push(K);
		B = Stack.Pop();
		P |= 0x20;
		A = [0x013C];
		A &= 0xDF;
		[0x4200] = A;
		[0x013C] = A;
		B = Stack.Pop();
		P = Stack.Pop();
		return;
	}

	public void L808306_Loop()
	{
		Stack.Push(P);
		Stack.Push(B);
		Stack.Push(K);
		B = Stack.Pop();
		P |= 0x20;
		A = [0x0154];

		if (Z == 1)
			return this.L808345_Done();

		[0x0154] = 0;
		[0x420B] = 0;
		[0x420C] = 0;
		P &= ~0x30;
		[0x0152] = 0;
		Y = 0x0000;
	}

	public void L808322_Loop()
	{
		// if (Y >= 0x100) Halt;
		C = 1; temp = Y - 0x0100;

		if (C == 0)
			return this.L808329_Skip();
	}

	public void L808327_Halt()
	{
		return this.L808327_Halt();
	}

	public void L808329_Skip()
	{
		// A = Table0155_DmaTransferQueue[Y] & 0xFF;
		A = [0x0155 + Y];
		A &= 0x00FF;

		// if (A >= 5) Halt;
		C = 1; temp = A - 0x0005;

		if (C == 0)
			return this.L808336_Skip();
	}

	public void L808334_Halt()
	{
		return this.L808334_Halt();
	}

	public void L808336_Skip()
	{
		// X = A * 2;
		A <<= 1;
		X = A;

		// Execute Function 0-4
		return [(0x833B + X)]();
	}

	public byte[] FunctionPointerTable80833B = new byte[]
	{
		0x45, 0x83,	// L808345
		0x4D, 0x83,	// L80834D
		0x8B, 0x83,	// L80838B
		0xD7, 0x83,	// L8083D7
		0x29, 0x84	// L808429
	}

	public void L808345_Done()
	{
		// Table0155_DmaTransferQueue[0] = 0;
		P |= 0x20;
		[0x0155] = 0;
		B = Stack.Pop();
		P = Stack.Pop();
		return;
	}

	public void L80834D()
	{
		P |= 0x20;
		A = [0x0156 + Y];
		[0x4312] = A;
		A = [0x0157 + Y];
		[0x4313] = A;
		A = [0x0158 + Y];
		[0x4314] = A;
		A = [0x0159 + Y];
		[0x4315] = A;
		A = [0x015A + Y];
		[0x4316] = A;
		A = [0x015B + Y];
		[0x2121] = A;
		[0x4310] = 0;
		A = 0x22;
		[0x4311] = A;
		A = 0x02;
		[0x420B] = A;
		P &= ~0x20;
		A = Y;
		C = 0;
		A += 0x0007 + C;
		Y = A;
		return this.L808322_Loop();
	}

	public void L80838B()
	{
		P |= 0x20;
		A = [0x0156 + Y];
		[0x4312] = A;
		A = [0x0157 + Y];
		[0x4313] = A;
		A = [0x0158 + Y];
		[0x4314] = A;
		A = [0x0159 + Y];
		[0x4315] = A;
		A = [0x015A + Y];
		[0x4316] = A;
		A = [0x015B + Y];
		[0x2115] = A;
		A = [0x015C + Y];
		[0x2116] = A;
		A = [0x015D + Y];
		[0x2117] = A;
		A = 0x01;
		[0x4310] = A;
		A = 0x18;
		[0x4311] = A;
		A = 0x02;
		[0x420B] = A;
		P &= ~0x20;
		A = Y;
		C = 0;
		A += 0x0009 + C;
		Y = A;
		return this.L808322_Loop();
	}

	public void L8083D7()
	{
		P |= 0x20;
		A = [0x0156 + Y];
		[0x4312] = A;
		A = [0x0157 + Y];
		[0x4313] = A;
		A = [0x0158 + Y];
		[0x4314] = A;
		A = [0x0159 + Y];
		[0x4315] = A;
		A = [0x015A + Y];
		[0x4316] = A;
		A = [0x015B + Y];
		[0x2115] = A;
		A = [0x015C + Y];
		[0x2116] = A;
		A = [0x015D + Y];
		[0x2117] = A;
		A = 0x81;
		[0x4310] = A;
		A = 0x39;
		[0x4311] = A;
		A = [0x2139];
		A = [0x213A];
		A = 0x02;
		[0x420B] = A;
		P &= ~0x20;
		A = Y;
		C = 0;
		A += 0x0009 + C;
		Y = A;
		return this.L808322_Loop();
	}

	public void L808429()
	{
		P |= 0x20;
		A = [0x0156 + Y];
		[0x4312] = A;
		A = [0x0157 + Y];
		[0x4313] = A;
		A = [0x0158 + Y];
		[0x4314] = A;
		A = [0x0159 + Y];
		[0x4315] = A;
		A = [0x015A + Y];
		[0x4316] = A;
		A = [0x015B + Y];
		[0x4310] = A;
		A = [0x015C + Y];
		[0x4311] = A;
		A = [0x015D + Y];
		[0x2115] = A;
		A = [0x015E + Y];
		[0x2116] = A;
		A = [0x015F + Y];
		[0x2117] = A;
		A = 0x02;
		[0x420B] = A;
		P &= ~0x20;
		A = Y;
		C = 0;
		A += 0x000B + C;
		Y = A;
		return this.L808322_Loop();
	}

	public void L80850F_SetMemory()
	{
		Stack.Push(P);
		Stack.Push(B);
		Stack.Push(K);
		B = Stack.Pop();
		P &= ~0x30;
	}

	public void L808515_Loop()
	{
		[0x7E0000 + X] = A;
		X++;
		X++;
		Y--;
		Y--;

		if (Z == 0)
			return this.L808515_Loop();

		B = Stack.Pop();
		P = Stack.Pop();
		return;
	}

	public void L8085A5()
	{
		Stack.Push(B);
		Stack.Push(K);
		B = Stack.Pop();
		Stack.Push(X);
		Stack.Push(Y);
		Stack.Push(A);
		Stack.Push(P);
		P &= ~0x20;
		P |= 0x10;
		X = [0x26];
		[0x4202] = X;
		X = [0x28];
		[0x4203] = X;
		Cpu.NOP();
		Cpu.NOP();
		Cpu.NOP();
		A = [0x4216];
		[0x2A] = A;
		X = [0x27];
		[0x4202] = X;
		X = [0x29];
		[0x4203] = X;
		Cpu.NOP();
		Cpu.NOP();
		Cpu.NOP();
		X = [0x4216];
		[0x2C] = X;
		Y = [0x4217];
		X = [0x27];
		[0x4202] = X;
		X = [0x28];
		[0x4203] = X;
		Cpu.NOP();
		Cpu.NOP();
		A = [0x2B];
		C = 0;
		A += [0x4216] + C;
		[0x2B] = A;

		if (C == 0)
			return this.L8085EE();

		Y++;
	}

	public void L8085EE()
	{
		X = [0x26];
		[0x4202] = X;
		X = [0x29];
		[0x4203] = X;
		Cpu.NOP();
		Cpu.NOP();
		A = [0x2B];
		C = 0;
		A += [0x4216] + C;
		[0x2B] = A;

		if (C == 0)
			return this.L808605();

		Y++;
	}

	public void L808605()
	{
		[0x2D] = Y;
		P = Stack.Pop();
		A = Stack.Pop();
		Y = Stack.Pop();
		X = Stack.Pop();
		B = Stack.Pop();
		return;
	}

	public void L80860D()
	{
		Stack.Push(P);
		Stack.Push(B);
		Stack.Push(K);
		B = Stack.Pop();
		P &= ~0x30;
		[0x2E] = 0;
		[0x30] = 0;
		[0x32] = 0;
		[0x34] = 0;
		P |= 0x10;
		X = [0x2A];
		this.L80863D();
		this.L80869C();
		X = [0x2B];
		this.L80863D();
		this.L80869C();
		X = [0x2C];
		this.L80863D();
		this.L80869C();
		X = [0x2D];
		this.L80863D();
		B = Stack.Pop();
		P = Stack.Pop();
		return;
	}

	public void L80863D()
	{
		[0x4202] = X;
		C = 0;
		X = [0x26];
		[0x4203] = X;
		Cpu.NOP();
		C = 0;
		A = [0x31];
		A += [0x4216] + C;
		[0x31] = A;
		A = [0x33];
		A += 0x0000 + C;
		[0x33] = A;
		P |= 0x20;
		A = [0x35];
		A += 0x00 + C;
		[0x35] = A;
		P &= ~0x20;
		X = [0x27];
		[0x4203] = X;
		Cpu.NOP();
		C = 0;
		A = [0x32];
		A += [0x4216] + C;
		[0x32] = A;
		A = [0x34];
		A += 0x0000 + C;
		[0x34] = A;
		X = [0x28];
		[0x4203] = X;
		Cpu.NOP();
		C = 0;
		A = [0x33];
		A += [0x4216] + C;
		[0x33] = A;
		P |= 0x20;
		A = [0x35];
		A += 0x00 + C;
		[0x35] = A;
		P &= ~0x20;
		X = [0x29];
		[0x4203] = X;
		Cpu.NOP();
		C = 0;
		A = [0x34];
		A += [0x4216] + C;
		[0x34] = A;
		return;
	}

	public void L80869C()
	{
		A = [0x2F];
		[0x2E] = A;
		A = [0x31];
		[0x30] = A;
		A = [0x33];
		[0x32] = A;
		X = [0x35];
		[0x34] = X;
		X = 0x00;
		[0x35] = X;
		return;
	}

	public void L8086B1()
	{
		Stack.Push(P);
		Stack.Push(B);
		Stack.Push(K);
		B = Stack.Pop();
		P &= ~0x30;
		[0x26] = 0;
		A = [0x2E];

		if (Z == 0)
			return this.L8086C1();

		[0x2C] = 0;
		return this.L8086D9();
	}

	public void L8086C1()
	{
		X = 0x0011;
		C = 0;
	}

	public void L8086C5()
	{
		Cpu.ROL(0x2C);
		X--;

		if (Z == 1)
			return this.L8086D9();

		Cpu.ROL(0x26);
		A = [0x26];

		if (Z == 1)
			return this.L8086C5();

		C = 1;
		A -= [0x2E] - !C;

		if (C == 0)
			return this.L8086C5();

		[0x26] = A;
		return this.L8086C5();
	}

	public void L8086D9()
	{
		B = Stack.Pop();
		P = Stack.Pop();
		return;
	}

	public void L8086DC()
	{
		Stack.Push(P);
		Stack.Push(B);
		Stack.Push(K);
		B = Stack.Pop();
		P &= ~0x30;
		[0x28] = 0;
		[0x26] = 0;
		A = [0x30];
		A |= [0x2E];

		if (Z == 0)
			return this.L8086F2();

		[0x2C] = 0;
		[0x2A] = 0;
		return this.L808719();
	}

	public void L8086F2()
	{
		X = 0x0021;
		C = 0;
		return this.L808712();
	}

	public void L8086F8()
	{
		Cpu.ROL(0x26);
		Cpu.ROL(0x28);

		if (Z == 0)
			return this.L808702();

		A = [0x26];

		if (Z == 1)
			return this.L808712();

	}

	public void L808702()
	{
		C = 1;
		A = [0x26];
		A -= [0x2E] - !C;
		Y = A;
		A = [0x28];
		A -= [0x30] - !C;

		if (C == 0)
			return this.L808712();

		[0x28] = A;
		[0x26] = Y;
	}

	public void L808712()
	{
		Cpu.ROL(0x2A);
		Cpu.ROL(0x2C);
		X--;

		if (Z == 0)
			return this.L8086F8();

	}

	public void L808719()
	{
		B = Stack.Pop();
		P = Stack.Pop();
		return;
	}

	public void L808744()

		Stack.Push(P);
		Stack.Push(B);

		B = Stack.Pop();
		P = Stack.Pop();
		return;
	}

	public void L8087A4_LoadRecords()
	{
		Stack.Push(P);
		P &= ~0x30;
		X = [0x0152];
		Y = 0x0000;

		// Table0155_DmaTransferQueue[X] = [Pointer00];
		P |= 0x20;
		A = [[0x00] + Y];
		Y++;
		[0x0155 + X] = A;
		A--;

		if (Z == 0)
			return this.L8087BB_Skip();

		return this.L808822_ReadDmaTransferRecord07();
	}

	public void L8087BB_Skip()
	{
		A--;

		if (Z == 0)
			return this.L8087C1();

		return this.L8087CD_ReadDmaTransferRecord09();
	}

	public void L8087C1()
	{
		A--;

		if (Z == 0)
			return this.L8087C7();

		return this.L8087CD_ReadDmaTransferRecord09();
	}

	public void L8087C7()
	{
		A--;

		if (Z == 0)
			return this.L8087CD_ReadDmaTransferRecord09();

		return this.L8087F3_ReadDmaTransferRecord0B();
	}

	public void L8087CD_ReadDmaTransferRecord09()
	{
		[0x015E + X] = 0;
		P &= ~0x20;
		A = [[0x00] + Y];
		[0x0156 + X] = A;
		Y++;
		Y++;
		A = [[0x00] + Y];
		[0x0158 + X] = A;
		Y++;
		Y++;
		A = [[0x00] + Y];
		[0x015A + X] = A;
		Y++;
		Y++;
		A = [[0x00] + Y];
		[0x015C + X] = A;
		A = X;
		C = 0;
		A += 0x0009 + C;
		return this.L80883F();
	}

	public void L8087F3_ReadDmaTransferRecord0B()

	public void L80883F()
	{
		[0x0152] = A;
		P |= 0x30;
		A = 0x01;
		[0x0154] = A;

	public void L808E91_Skip()
	{
		// Word0261 = Word0259 + Word025D;
		A = [0x0259];
		C = 0;
		A += [0x025D] + C;
		[0x0261] = A;

		// Word0263 = Word025B + Word025F
		A = [0x025B];
		C = 0;
		A += [0x025F] + C;
		[0x0263] = A;

		P = Stack.Pop();
		return;
	}
